) AS [d0] ON [a].[DoctorId] = [d0].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [u].[Id], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[Email], [u].[FirstName], [u].[IsActive], [u].[LastName], [u].[OrganizationId], [u].[PasswordHash], [u].[Phone], [u].[RefreshToken], [u].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [u].[Role], [u].[SelectedClinicId], [u].[UpdatedAt]
    FROM [Users] AS [u]
) AS [u0] ON [d0].[UserId] = [u0].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[Address], [p].[BloodGroup], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[DateOfBirth], [p].[EmergencyContact], [p].[Gender], [p].[IsActive], [p].[MedicalHistory], [p].[OrganizationId], [p].[PatientCode], [p].[UpdatedAt], [p].[UserId]
    FROM [Patients] AS [p]
) AS [p0] ON [a].[PatientId] = [p0].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [u1].[Id], [u1].[CreatedAt], [u1].[Email], [u1].[FirstName], [u1].[IsActive], [u1].[LastName], [u1].[OrganizationId], [u1].[PasswordHash], [u1].[Phone], [u1].[RefreshToken], [u1].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [u1].[Role], [u1].[SelectedClinicId], [u1].[UpdatedAt]
    FROM [Users] AS [u1]
) AS [u2] ON [p0].[UserId] = [u2].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[Address], [c].[Code], [c].[ContactEmail], [c].[ContactPhone], [c].[CreatedAt], [c].[IsActive], [c].[Name], [c].[OrganizationId], [c].[UpdatedAt]
    FROM [Clinics] AS [c]
) AS [c0] ON [a].[ClinicId] = [c0].[Id]

FROM [Appointments] AS [a]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[ConsultationFeeInPerson], [d].[ConsultationFeeTele], [d].[CreatedAt], [d].[ExperienceYears], [d].[FollowupFeeInPerson], [d].[FollowupFeeTele], [d].[IsActive], [d].[OrganizationId], [d].[Qualification], [d].[RegistrationNumber], [d].[Specialization], [d].[UpdatedAt], [d].[UserId]
    FROM [DoctorProfiles] AS [d]
) AS [d0] ON [a].[DoctorId] = [d0].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [u].[Id], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[Email], [u].[FirstName], [u].[IsActive], [u].[LastName], [u].[OrganizationId], [u].[PasswordHash], [u].[Phone], [u].[RefreshToken], [u].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [u].[Role], [u].[SelectedClinicId], [u].[UpdatedAt]
    FROM [Users] AS [u]
) AS [u0] ON [d0].[UserId] = [u0].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[Address], [p].[BloodGroup], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[DateOfBirth], [p].[EmergencyContact], [p].[Gender], [p].[IsActive], [p].[MedicalHistory], [p].[OrganizationId], [p].[PatientCode], [p].[UpdatedAt], [p].[UserId]
    FROM [Patients] AS [p]
) AS [p0] ON [a].[PatientId] = [p0].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [u1].[Id], [u1].[CreatedAt], [u1].[Email], [u1].[FirstName], [u1].[IsActive], [u1].[LastName], [u1].[OrganizationId], [u1].[PasswordHash], [u1].[Phone], [u1].[RefreshToken], [u1].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [u1].[Role], [u1].[SelectedClinicId], [u1].[UpdatedAt]
    FROM [Users] AS [u1]
) AS [u2] ON [p0].[UserId] = [u2].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[Address], [c].[Code], [c].[ContactEmail], [c].[ContactPhone], [c].[CreatedAt], [c].[IsActive], [c].[Name], [c].[OrganizationId], [c].[UpdatedAt]
    FROM [Clinics] AS [c]
) AS [c0] ON [a].[ClinicId] = [c0].[Id]
WHERE [a].[ClinicId] = @__request_ClinicId_Value_0 AND [a].[AppointmentDate] = @__request_Date_Value_1
ORDER BY [a].[AppointmentDate], [a].[TokenNumber]
